class=\"btop\">Helping Your Child Read and Write</div>\n<div class=\"bod2\"><br>Families are their children's first teachers. As a family member you begin teaching your babies about language as you welcome them into the world with smiles and caring words. &nbsp; <a href=\"//resources.raisingourkids.com/read/\" class=\"copy\">Read more ...</a> \n<a href=\"//resources.raisingourkids.com/read/\"><img src=\"resources/read/images/preschool-learn-read.gif\" alt=\"Help your child learn to read and write\" width=\"133\" height=\"176\" border=\"0\" align=\"right\"></a>\n<br><br>\nMost of the activities here are simple to do with materials found in your home or at the library.
